## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t, which is the central problem in mathematical population ecology. The relationship likely involves density-dependent feedback mechanisms where growth rate depends on current population level.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, Malthusian model)
- Logistic growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Theta-logistic model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population)
- Von Bertalanffy growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolic vs catabolic scaling)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P (density-dependent birth minus death)
- Seasonal Malthusian: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) (time-varying growth rate)
- Seasonal logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (logistic with seasonal forcing)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional-order density dependence)
- Richards growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (generalized growth curve derivative)
- Quadratic density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (polynomial density effects)
- Time-decaying growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponentially changing environment)
- Harvesting model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth with constant harvesting)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope Γ¶Ê Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects Γ¶Ê Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay Γ¶Ê Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior Γ¶Ê Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects Γ¶Ê Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear proportionality to P Γ¶Ê Exponential/Malthusian regime: dP_dt = c*P indicates density-independent growth
- Quadratic P term (P*(1-P/K)) Γ¶Ê Logistic density-dependent regulation with carrying capacity
- Cubic polynomial in P (P*(P-A)*(1-P/K)) Γ¶Ê Allee effect with both lower and upper critical thresholds
- Logarithmic coupling log(K/P)*P Γ¶Ê Gompertz-type asymmetric growth, slower approach to carrying capacity
- Difference of power laws (P^a - P^b) Γ¶Ê Von Bertalanffy metabolic scaling between anabolism and catabolism
- Trigonometric modulation sin(c*t) multiplied by growth term Γ¶Ê Seasonal or periodic environmental forcing
- Ratio P/(1+c*P) structure in growth Γ¶Ê Contest competition where per-capita resources saturate
- Negative constant term independent of P Γ¶Ê Constant-rate harvesting or immigration effects
- Product of multiple linear factors in P Γ¶Ê Multiple equilibria and bistability in population dynamics
- Exponential time dependence in coefficients Γ¶Ê Gradual environmental degradation or improvement over time
